Gerenciamento de sess√£o
Neste t√≥pico ser√£o apresentados os comandos utilizados para administra√ß√£o da sess√£o nos equipamentos. Eles s√£o importantes e necess√°rios para iniciar, analisar e finalizar a comunica√ß√£o via requisi√ß√µes HTTP com os dispositivos.

POST
Login
192.168.0.129/login.fcgi
Comando para criar uma sess√£o que √© necess√°ria para todos os outros comandos, exceto session_is_valid. O m√©todo HTTP usado para o envio dos dados √© o POST.

HEADERS
Content-Type
application/json

Body
raw
{
    "login": "admin",
    "password": "admin"
}

Example Request
Sucesso

python
import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/login.fcgi"

payload = json.dumps({
  "login": "admin",
  "password": "admin"
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)

200 OK

import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/get_vpn_information.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

print(response.text)
200 OK

python
import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/execute_actions.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "actions": [
    {
      "action": "sec_box",
      "parameters": "id=65793, reason=3"
    }
  ]
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)

url = "192.168.0.129/create_objects.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "object": "time_zones",
  "values": [
    {
      "name": "Fim de Semana"
    }
  ]
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)
Example Response
Body
Headers (0)
No response body
This request doesn't return any response body

import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/create_objects.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "object": "user_groups",
  "fields": [
    "user_id",
    "group_id"
  ],
  "values": [
    {
      "user_id": 1,
      "group_id": 1
    }
  ]
})

  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

python
import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/report_generate.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "order": [
    "ascending",
    "name"
  ],
  "where": {
    "users": {},
    "groups": {},
    "time_zones": {}
  },
  "object": "users",
  "delimiter": ";",
  "line_break": "\\r\\n",
  "header": "Nome (Usu√°rio);C√≥digo (Usu√°rio)",
  "file_name": "",
  "join": "LEFT",
  "columns": [
    {
      "type": "object_field",
      "object": "users",
      "field": "name",
      "format": {
        "adjustment": 1,
        "width": 50,
        "fill": " ",
        "format": "%s"
      }
    },
    {
      "type": "object_field",
      "object": "users",
      "field": "id",
      "format": {
        "adjustment": 2,
        "width": 5,
        "fill": "0",
        "format": "%s"
      }
    }
  ]
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)
Example Response
Body
Headers (0)
No response body
This request doesn't return any response body

import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/set_configuration.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "general": {
    "ssh_enabled": "0"
  }
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)
200 OK

import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/get_configuration.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "general": [
    "online",
    "beep_enabled",
    "relay1_enabled",
    "relay1_timeout",
    "relay1_auto_close",
    "relay2_enabled",
    "relay2_timeout",
    "relay2_auto_close",
    "bell_enabled",
    "bell_relay",
    "local_identification",
    "exception_mode",
    "language",
    "daylight_savings_time_start",
    "daylight_savings_time_end",
    "auto_reboot"
  ],
  "mifare": [
    "byte_order"
  ],
  "w_in0": [
    "byte_order"
  ],
  "w_out0": [
    "data"
  ],
  "alarm": [
    "siren_enabled"
  ],
  "identifier": [
    "verbose_logging",
    "log_type",
    "multi_factor_authentication"
  ],
  "bio_id": [
    "similarity_threshold_1ton"
  ],
  "online_client": [
    "server_id",
    "extract_template",
    "max_request_attempts"
  ],
  "bio_module": [
    "var_min"
  ],
  "monitor": [
    "path",
    "hostname",
    "port",
    "request_timeout"
  ],
  "push_server": [
    "push_request_timeout",
    "push_request_period",
    "push_remote_address"
  ]
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)

python
import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/set_configuration.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "general": {
    "language": "pt_BR"
  }
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'

url = "192.168.0.129/set_configuration.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "hid_reader": {
    "ignore_facility": "1"
  }
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)
200 OK
Example Response
Body
Headers (7)
json
{}

python
import requests
import json

url = "192.168.0.129/user_destroy_image.fcgi?session="

payload = json.dumps({
  "user_ids": [
    27,
    28
  ]
})
headers = {
  'Content-Type': 'application/json'
}

response = requests.request("POST", url, headers=headers, data=payload)

print(response.text)

})
